\DIFadd{Push $n\to\infty$ in Lemma~\ref{lem:equiv_n_nv} along the lines of
\mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
\cite[Proof of Proposition~5.6]{chcora}}\hskip0pt%DIFAUXCMD
.
}

\begin{proof}[Proof of Proposition~\textup{\ref{PRO:equiv}}]
\DIFadd{Take $u_0$ as in \eqref{equiv-0}. Denote by
$z\in X^{s',b}(0,T_{\dl,R})$ the \eqref{z1} solution with data
$z_0:=\Gc_\dl[u_0]$ (Proposition~\ref{prop:lwp_rnv}), and let
$u\in X^{s',b}(0,T)$ be the maximal \eqref{eq:NV} solution issued
from $u_0$
\mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
\cite{angelopolous,kazeykinamunoz1,kazeykinamunoz2}}\hskip0pt%DIFAUXCMD
. Lemma~\ref{lem:equiv_n_nv}
furnishes $u_n,z_n$ with $u_n(0)=u_0$ and
$z_n(0)=\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_0]$. The proof reduces to the pair of
convergences
}\begin{align}
\label{eq:conv_zn}
z_n &\to z \quad\text{in}\quad C([0,T_{\dl,R}]; H^{s'-1}(\R^2)),
\\
\label{eq:conv_Gun}
\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_n] &\to \Gc_\dl[u]
\quad\text{in}\quad C([0,T\wedge T_{\dl,R}); H^{s'-1}(\R^2)).
\end{align}
\DIFadd{Granted \eqref{eq:conv_zn}-\eqref{eq:conv_Gun}, the identity
\eqref{eq:equiv_n_nv} yields $\Gc_\dl[u(t)]=z(t)$ in $H^{s'-1}$ on
$[0,T\wedge T_{\dl,R})$. The $L^\infty_t H^{s'}$ control on $z$
provided by Proposition~\ref{prop:lwp_rnv} and
Remark~\ref{remark:persistence}, transferred through
Lemma~\ref{LEM:D} as
$\|u(t)\|_{H^{s'}}\le \|z\|_{L^\infty_t H^{s'}}/(1-\eps)$,
prevents }\DIFaddend $u$ \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{from blowing up before $T_{\dl,R}$. Thus
$T\ge T_{\dl,R}$ and the identity persists to all of
$[0,T_{\dl,R}]$, which is \eqref{equiv-1}.
}

\smallskip
\noindent\emph{\DIFadd{Proof of \eqref{eq:conv_zn}.}}\DIFadd{\
Subtracting the Duhamel formulations of \eqref{z1} and
\eqref{eq:GNV_n_dens} splits $z(t)-z_n(t)$ into three pieces:
}\begin{align*}
z(t)-z_n(t)
&= U(t)(\Gc_\dl-\Gc_{\dl,n})[u_0]
+ \sum_{j,\TT,\l}\!\int_0^t\! U(t-t')
\big[\Ncal_\l(\TT;z)-\Ncal_{\l,n}(\TT;z)\big]\,dt'
\\
&\quad
+ \sum_{j,\TT,\l}\!\int_0^t\! U(t-t')
\big[\Ncal_{\l,n}(\TT;z)-\Ncal_{\l,n}(\TT;z_n)\big]\,dt'.
\end{align*}
\DIFadd{Proposition~\ref{prop:bourgL2} (applied to the truncated multipliers,
which it covers without change) together with the smallness of $z$
}\DIFaddend and $z_n$ \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{converges to the \eqref{z1} solution $z$. This is an easy consequence of the multilinear estimates }\DIFdelend in \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{$X^{s',b}$. Then, taking the
limit in $n$ in the relation $\mathcal{G}_{\delta,n}[u_n]=z_n$, }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{$L^\infty_t H^s$ bounds the third sum by
$\tfrac12\|z-z_n\|_{X^{s'-1,b}(0,T_{\dl,R})}$, which is absorbed.
For the data term, the two presentations
$u_0=\Gc_\dl[u_0]+\D[\Gc_\dl[u_0],\Gc_\dl[u_0]]
=\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_0]+\mathbf{P}_n\D[\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_0],\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_0]]$
of $u_0$ ($\D$ as in \eqref{eq:gauge}), combined with the
small-Lipschitz estimate on $\D$ inside the proof of
Lemma~\ref{LEM:D}, give
}\[
\|(\Gc_\dl-\Gc_{\dl,n})[u_0]\|_{H^{s'-1}}
\lesssim \|\mathbf{P}_{>n}\D[\Gc_\dl[u_0],\Gc_\dl[u_0]]\|_{H^{s'-1}}
\lesssim n^{-1}\|\D[\Gc_\dl[u_0],\Gc_\dl[u_0]]\|_{H^{s'}}
\to 0.
\]
\DIFadd{Finally, $\Ncal_\l(\TT)-\Ncal_{\l,n}(\TT)$ decomposes into finitely
many operators of the same multilinear form as $\Ncal_{\l,n}$,
each picking up an indicator $\ind_{|\xi_\bul|>n}$ on some node;
Proposition~\ref{prop:bourgL2} disposes of each, and trading the
extra $\jap{\xi_\bul}$ against the $H^{s'-1}\hookrightarrow H^{s'}$
upgrade (which $z$ provides uniformly) creates a saving
$\jap{\xi_\bul}^{-1}\le n^{-1}$. The mechanism is the one of
\mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
\cite{chcora}}\hskip0pt%DIFAUXCMD
; the only NV twist is that the indicator now lives on
$\R^2$. Summing the three contributions establishes
\eqref{eq:conv_zn}.
}

\smallskip
\noindent\emph{\DIFadd{Proof of \eqref{eq:conv_Gun}.}}\DIFadd{\
The intermediate step is
}\begin{equation}\label{eq:conv_un}
u_n \to u \quad\text{in}\quad C([0,T\wedge T_{\dl,R}); H^{s'-1}(\R^2)).
\end{equation}
\DIFadd{Working on sub-intervals of length $T_*$ controlled only by
$M:=2\|u_0\|_{H^{s'}}$, the high-regularity bilinear estimates
\mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
\cite{angelopolous,kazeykinamunoz1,kazeykinamunoz2} }\hskip0pt%DIFAUXCMD
furnish
}\[
\|u_n-u\|_{X^{s'-1,b}(0,T_*)}
\le \tfrac12\|u_n-u\|_{X^{s'-1,b}(0,T_*)}
+ \frac{C}{n}\,T_*^\theta\,\|u\|_{X^{s',b}(0,T_*)}^2,
\]
\DIFadd{the factor $n^{-1}$ originating from upgrading $\mathbf{P}_{>n}$ from
$s'-1$ to $s'$. Chaining these sub-intervals yields
\eqref{eq:conv_un} and, together with \eqref{eq:bounds_un}, }\DIFaddend the
\DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{proof is finished}\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{auxiliary bound $\|u\|_{L^\infty_t H^s}<3R$ on
$[0,T\wedge T_{\dl,R})$.
}

\DIFadd{The identity \eqref{eq:conv_Gun} follows by inserting the two
representations
}\[
u_n=\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_n]+\mathbf{P}_n\D[\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_n],\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_n]],
\qquad
u=\Gc_\dl[u]+\D[\Gc_\dl[u],\Gc_\dl[u]],
\]
\DIFadd{into
}\[
\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_n]-\Gc_\dl[u]
= (u_n-u)
- \mathbf{P}_n\big(\D[\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_n],\Gc_{\dl,n}[u_n]]
- \D[\Gc_\dl[u],\Gc_\dl[u]]\big)
- \mathbf{P}_{>n}\D[\Gc_\dl[u],\Gc_\dl[u]],
\]
\DIFadd{and treating the three summands by \eqref{eq:conv_un}, by the
small-Lipschitz estimate on $\D$ coming from the proof of
Lemma~\ref{LEM:D}, and by the $H^{s'}$-control of
$\D[\Gc_\dl[u],\Gc_\dl[u]]$, respectively}\DIFaddend .
\end{proof}

\DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{In particular, for smooth data in
}%DIFDELCMD < $$
%DIFDELCMD < B_R=\{u\in H^s(\R^2) : \|u\|_{H^s}< R \},
%DIFDELCMD < $$
%DIFDELCMD < %%%
\DIFdel{the \eqref{eq:NV} is conjugate (via $\Gc_{\delta}$) to }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \subsection{\DIFadd{Conclusion of Theorem~\ref{thm:main_intro}}}

\DIFadd{Proposition~\ref{PRO:equiv} states that, restricted to the ball
$B_R:=\{u_0\in H^s(\R^2):\|u_0\|_{H^s}<R\}$ and the uniform window
$[0,T_{\dl,R}]$, the smooth \eqref{eq:NV} flow
($u_0\in H^{s'}(\R^2)\cap B_R$, $s'\gg 1$) is the conjugate, by the
analytic map $\Gc_\dl$ from Lemma~\ref{LEM:D}, of }\DIFaddend the \eqref{z1}
flow\DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{, with a uniform local time of existence. Since both the gauge transform $\Gc_\delta$, its inverse $\Gc_{\dl}^{-1}$, and the \eqref{z1}-flow have continuous (and even analytic) extensions }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{. The latter admits a continuous --- indeed analytic ---
extension from $H^{s'}\cap B_R$ to the full ball $B_R\subset H^s(\R^2)$,
via Proposition~\ref{prop:lwp_rnv} together with the multilinear
estimates of Proposition~\ref{prop:bourgL2}. Continuity of $\Gc_\dl$
and $\Gc_\dl^{-1}$ on $B_R\subset H^s$ (Lemma~\ref{LEM:D}) makes the
composition
$\Gc_\dl^{-1}\circ\Phi^{\Gc_\dl\text{-NV}}\circ\Gc_\dl$
a continuous prolongation of the \eqref{eq:NV} flow from
$\mathcal{S}(\R^2)\cap B_R$ }\DIFaddend to $B_R$, \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{this concludes the proof of
Theorem \ref{thm:main_intro}.
}\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{with the existence time
$T_{\dl,R}$ uniform across the ball. Density of
$\mathcal{S}(\R^2)$ in $H^s(\R^2)$ identifies this extension with
the limit of the smooth solutions
$u_n\in C([0,T_{\dl,R}];H^{s'})$ of
\mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
\cite{angelopolous,kazeykinamunoz1,kazeykinamunoz2}}\hskip0pt%DIFAUXCMD
; analyticity is
inherited from the factors. Theorem~\ref{thm:main_intro} is
proved.
}\qed
\DIFaddend 



\appendix

\section{Improved local well-posedness for \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{$s>-\frac{3}{4}$}\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \texorpdfstring{$s>-\frac{3}{4}$}{s>-3/4}\DIFaddend }\DIFaddbegin \label{sec:s-34}
\DIFaddend 

In this short appendix, we extend the well-posedness result in $H^s, s>-\frac{3}{4},$ of Adams and Grünrock for the zero-energy \eqref{eq:NV} to the nonzero case. In particular, we are able to improve the properties of the \eqref{eq:NV} flow constructed in Theorem \ref{thm:main_intro}. 


\begin{theorem}\label{thm:s-34}
Fix $E\in \R$ and $s>-\frac{3}{4}$. Given $u_0\in H^s(\R^2)$, there exists $T>0$ and a unique $u\in X^{s,b}_T$ strong integral solution to \eqref{eq:NV} with initial data $u_0$. Moreover, the data-to-solution map is analytic.
\end{theorem}


As before, using the scaling invariance, it suffices to prove Theorem \ref{thm:s-34} for $|E|<1$. We define the bilinear operator associated with the \eqref{eq:NV} nonlinearity (see \eqref{eq:NV2}):
$$
B[u_1,u_2]^\wedge(\xi):=\int_{\xi=\xi_1+\xi_2} K\Phi_0u_1(\xi_1)u_2(\xi_2)d\xi_1
$$
Then, using the standard theory of Fourier restriction norm spaces (\cite{bourg1,bourg2}, see also the monographs \cite{linaresponce, tao_book}), the proof of Theorem \ref{thm:s-34} follows from 

\begin{proposition}\DIFaddbegin \label{prop:bilin_s-34}
\DIFaddend Fix $E\in \R$ and $s>-\frac{3}{4}$. Then
\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \begin{equation}\label{eq:bilin_s-34}
%DIFDELCMD < \left\| B[u_1,u_2]\right\|_{X^{s,-\frac{1}{2}+}}\lesssim \|u_1\|_{X^{s,\frac{1}{2}+}}\|u_2\|_{X^{s,\frac{1}{2}+}}
%DIFDELCMD < \end{equation}%%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \begin{equation}\label{eq:bilin_s-34}
\left\| B[u_1,u_2]\right\|_{X^{s,-\frac{1}{2}+}}\lesssim \|u_1\|_{X^{s,\frac{1}{2}+}}\|u_2\|_{X^{s,\frac{1}{2}+}}.
\end{equation}\DIFaddend 
\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < 

%DIFDELCMD < %%%
\DIFdelend \end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
First, we decompose $B$ as
\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \begin{align*}
%DIFDELCMD < B[u_1,u_2]^\wedge(\xi)&=\int_{\xi=\xi_1+\xi_2} K\Phi\mathbbm{1}_{A^c}u_1(\xi_1)u_2(\xi_2)d\xi_1 \\&\qquad+ \int_{\xi=\xi_1+\xi_2} K(\Phi_0\mathbbm{1}_A -E\Phi_E\mathbbm{1}_{A^c})u_1(\xi_1)u_2(\xi_2)d\xi_1
%DIFDELCMD < \end{align*}%%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \begin{align*}
B[u_1,u_2]^\wedge(\xi)&=\int_{\xi=\xi_1+\xi_2} K\Phi\mathbbm{1}_{A^c}u_1(\xi_1)u_2(\xi_2)d\xi_1 \\&\qquad+ \int_{\xi=\xi_1+\xi_2} K(\Phi_0\mathbbm{1}_A -E\Phi_E\mathbbm{1}_{A^c})u_1(\xi_1)u_2(\xi_2)d\xi_1.
\end{align*}\DIFaddend 
The bilinear estimate for the last term \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{as }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{has }\DIFaddend already been shown in Proposition \ref{prop:bourgL2} (it corresponds to the \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{type }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{Type }\DIFaddend $\I$ term). For the remaining term, we \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{will }\DIFdelend use Lemma \ref{lem:fre_bi}-(i) (together with Lemma \ref{lem:eta1}) and prove the necessary frequency-restricted estimates.

To simplify the exposition, we take $-\frac{3}{4}<s<-\frac{1}{2}$ and consider only the worst-case scenario $|\xi_1|\sim |\xi_2|\gtrsim |\xi|$. For \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{fixed $\alpha, M\in \R$ with $|\alpha|\lesssim M>1$}\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{$\alpha\in\R$ and $M>1$ with $|\alpha|\lesssim M$}\DIFaddend , we bound
\begin{align}
\frac{\jap{\xi}^{2s}|K\Phi|^2}{\jap{\xi_1}^{2s+0-}\jap{\xi_2}^{2s}}\mathbbm{1}_{A^c}\ind_{|\Phi-\alpha|<M}&\lesssim |\alpha|\frac{\jap{\xi}^{2s+1}}{\jap{\xi_1}^{2s+1-}\jap{\xi_2}^{2s+1}}\mathbbm{1}_{A^c}\ind_{|\Phi-\alpha|<M}\\&\lesssim |\alpha|\frac{1}{\jap{\xi_1}^{2s+1-}\jap{\xi_2}^{2s+1}}\mathbbm{1}_{A^c}\ind_{|\Phi-\alpha|<M}.
\end{align}
For $\xi_2$ fixed, if $\xi_1\not\simeq \pm\xi$, then, by Lemma \ref{lem:prop_resonance}-(i),
$$
|\nabla_{\xi_1}\Phi|\gtrsim |\xi_1|^2
$$
and
\begin{align}
\int \frac{1}{\jap{\xi_1}^{2s+1-}\jap{\xi_2}^{2s+1}}\ind_{|\Phi-\alpha|<M}d\xi_1 \lesssim \int \frac{1}{\jap{\zeta_1}^{4s+4-}}\ind_{|\Phi-\alpha|<M}d\Phi d\zeta_1 \lesssim M,
\end{align}
for $s>-\frac{3}{4}$. On the other hand, if $\xi_1\simeq \pm \xi$, then all frequencies are comparable and, by Lemma \ref{lem:prop_resonance}-(ii), there exists a change of coordinates $\xi_1\mapsto q_1$, with jacobian $\sim |\xi_2|^2$, such that
$$
\Phi=|\xi_2|^3\Re q_1^2-\phi(\xi_2).
$$
Hence
\begin{align*}
\int_{|q_1|<1} \jap{\xi_2}^{-4s+0+}\ind_{||\xi_2|^3\Re q_1^2-\phi(\xi_2)-\alpha|<M}dq_1 \lesssim \jap{\xi_2}^{-4s-3+0+}M\lesssim M,
\end{align*}
for $s>-\frac{3}{4}$.
\smallskip
For $\xi_1$ (or $\xi$) fixed, the proof follows the same lines \textit{mutatis mutandis}. Thus
\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \begin{equation}\label{eq:final_appendix}
%DIFDELCMD < \sup_{k=\emptyset, 1, 2}\sup_{\xi_k}\int_{\xi=\xi_1+\xi_2}
%DIFDELCMD <         \frac{|K\Phi|^2\jap{\xi}^{2s}}{\jap{\xi_{1}}^{2s+0-}\jap{\xi_{2}}^{2s}}\ind_{A^c}\mathbbm{1}_{|\Phi(\<1>)-\alpha|<M} d\xi_{\l} \lesssim \jap{\alpha}M
%DIFDELCMD <     \end{equation}%%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \begin{equation}\label{eq:final_appendix}
\sup_{k\in\{\emptyset, 1, 2\}}\sup_{\xi_k}\int_{\xi=\xi_1+\xi_2}
        \frac{|K\Phi|^2\jap{\xi}^{2s}}{\jap{\xi_{1}}^{2s+0-}\jap{\xi_{2}}^{2s}}\ind_{A^c}\mathbbm{1}_{|\Phi(\<1>)-\alpha|<M}\, d\xi_{k} \lesssim \jap{\alpha}\,M,
    \end{equation}\DIFaddend 
and \eqref{eq:bilin_s-34} follows from Lemma \ref{lem:fre_bi}-(i) and Lemma \ref{lem:eta1}.
\end{proof}



%DIF <  \begin{proposition}[Equivalence between NV and the gauged NV at high regularity]\label{prop:equiv} Fix $s\gg 1$ and $u_0\in H^s(\R^2)$ with $\|u_0\|_{H^s}<R$. Then the following are equivalent:
\DIFaddbegin \bibliographystyle{plain}
